text">\xe6\x97\xa5\xe6\x9c\xac\xe5\x9c\x8b</span></span></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<table class="collapsible collapsed" style="padding:0;border:none;margin:-3px;width:auto;min-width:100%;font-size:100%;clear:none;float:none;background-color:transparent"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" href="/wiki/Hepburn_romanization" title="Hepburn romanization">Revised Hepburn</a></th><td>\nNippon-koku<br />Nihon-koku</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr style="display:none"><td colspan="2">\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Japan</b> (<a href="/wiki/Japanese_language" title="Japanese language">Japanese</a>: <span lang="ja">\xe6\x97\xa5\xe6\x9c\xac</span>; <i>Nippon</i> <small></small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Japanese" title="Help:IPA/Japanese">[\xc9\xb2ippo\xc9\xb4]</a></span> or <i>Nihon</i> <small></small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Japanese" title="Help:IPA/Japanese">[\xc9\xb2iho\xc9\xb4]</a></span>; formally <span lang="ja" title="Japanese language text">\xe6\x97\xa5\xe6\x9c\xac\xe5\x9b\xbd</span> <i><span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Ja-nippon_nihonkoku.ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20" /></a>&#160;</span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/86/Ja-nippon_nihonkoku.ogg" class="internal" title="Ja-nippon nihonkoku.ogg">Nippon-koku</a></span></span></i> or <i>Nihon-koku</i>, lit. "State of Japan") is an <a href="/wiki/Island_country" title="Island country">island country</a> in <a href="/wiki/East_Asia" title="East Asia">East Asia</a>. Located in the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>, it lies off the eastern coast of the Asian mainland and stretches from the <a href="/wiki/Sea_of_Okhotsk" title="Sea of Okhotsk">Sea of Okhotsk</a> in the north to the <a href="/wiki/East_China_Sea" title="East China Sea">East China Sea</a> and <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> in the southwest.\n<span style="font-size: small;"><span id="coordinates"><a href="/wiki/Geographic_coordinate_system" title="Geographic coordinate system">Coordinates</a>: <span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion"><a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/geohack/geohack.php?pagename=Japan&amp;params=35_N_136_E_type:country_region:JP"><span class="geo-default"><span class="geo-dms" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location"><span class="latitude">35\xc2\xb0N</span> <span class="longitude">136\xc2\xb0E</span></span></span><span class="geo-multi-punct">&#xfeff; / &#xfeff;</span><span class="geo-nondefault"><span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">35\xc2\xb0N 136\xc2\xb0E</span><span style="display:none">&#xfeff; / <span class="geo">35; 136</span></span></span></a></span></span></span>\nThe <a href="/wiki/Kanji" title="Kanji">kanji</a> that make up <a href="/wiki/Names_of_Japan" title="Names of Japan">Japan\'s name</a> mean "sun origin", and it is often called the "Land of the Rising Sun". Japan is a <a href="/wiki/Stratovolcano" title="Stratovolcano">stratovolcanic</a> <a href="/wiki/Archipelago" title="Archipelago">archipelago</a> consisting of about <a href="/wiki/List_of_islands_of_Japan" title="List of islands of Japan">6,852 islands</a>. The four largest are <a href="/wiki/Honshu" title="Honshu">Honshu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hokkaido" title="Hokkaido">Hokkaido</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kyushu" title="Kyushu">Kyushu</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Shikoku" title="Shikoku">Shikoku</a>, which make up about ninety-seven percent of Japan\'s land area and often are referred to as home islands. The country is divided into 47 <a href="/wiki/Prefectures_of_Japan" title="Prefectures of Japan">prefectures</a> in eight <a href="/wiki/List_of_regions_of_Japan" title="List of regions of Japan">regions</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Hokkaido" title="Hokkaido">Hokkaido</a> being the northernmost prefecture and <a href="/wiki/Okinawa_Prefecture" title="Okinawa Prefecture">Okinawa</a> being the southernmost one. The population of 127&#160;million is the <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_population" class="mw-redirect" title="List of countries by population">world\'s tenth largest</a>. <a href="/wiki/Japanese_people" title="Japanese people">Japanese people</a> make up 98.5% of Japan\'s total population. About 9.1 million people live in <a href="/wiki/Tokyo" title="Tokyo">Tokyo</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Capital_of_Japan" title="Capital of Japan">capital of Japan</a>.\n</p><p>Archaeological research indicates that Japan was inhabited as early as the <a href="/wiki/Upper_Paleolithic" title="Upper Paleolithic">Upper Paleolithic</a> period. The first written mention of Japan is in <a href="/wiki/History_of_China" title="History of China">Chinese history</a> texts from the 1st century AD. Influence from other regions, mainly <a href="/wiki/Imperial_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Imperial China">China</a>, followed by periods of isolation, particularly from Western Europe, has characterized <a href="/wiki/History_of_Japan" title="History of Japan">Japan\'s history</a>.\n</p><p>From the 12th century until 1868, Japan was ruled by successive feudal military <i><a href="/wiki/Sh%C5%8Dgun" title="Sh\xc5\x8dgun">sh\xc5\x8dguns</a></i> who ruled in the name of the <a href="/wiki/Emperor_of_Japan" title="Emperor of Japan">Emperor</a>. Japan entered into a long <a href="/wiki/Sakoku" title="Sakoku">period of isolation</a> in the early 17th century, which was ended in 1853 when a United States fleet <a href="/wiki/Bakumatsu" title="Bakumatsu">pressured Japan</a> to open to the West. After nearly two decades of internal conflict and insurrection, the Imperial Court <a href="/wiki/Meiji_oligarchy" title="Meiji oligarchy">regained</a> its political power in 1868 through the help of several clans from <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%8Dsh%C5%AB_Domain" title="Ch\xc5\x8dsh\xc5\xab Domain">Ch\xc5\x8dsh\xc5\xab</a> and <a href="/wiki/Satsuma_Domain" title="Satsuma Domain">Satsuma</a>\xe2\x80\x94and the <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">Empire of Japan</a> was established. In the late 19th and early 20th centuries, victories in the <a href="/wiki/First_Sino-Japanese_War" title="First Sino-Japanese War">First Sino-Japanese War</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Russo-Japanese_War" title="Russo-Japanese War">Russo-Japanese War</a> and <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a> allowed Japan to expand its empire during a period of increasing <a href="/wiki/Japanese_militarism" title="Japanese militarism">militarism</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Second_Sino-Japanese_War" title="Second Sino-Japanese War">Second Sino-Japanese War</a> of 1937 expanded into part of <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a> in 1941, which came to an <a href="/wiki/End_of_World_War_II_in_Asia" title="End of World War II in Asia">end in 1945</a> following the <a href="/wiki/Atomic_bombings_of_Hiroshima_and_Nagasaki" title="Atomic bombings of Hiroshima and Nagasaki">atomic bombings of Hiroshima and Nagasaki</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Surrender_of_Japan" title="Surrender of Japan">Japanese surrender</a>. Since adopting its revised <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Japan" title="Constitution of Japan">constitution</a> on May 3, 1947, during the <a href="/wiki/Occupation_of_Japan" title="Occupation of Japan">occupation</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Commander_for_the_Allied_Powers" title="Supreme Commander for the Allied Powers">SCAP</a>, Japan has maintained a <a href="/wiki/Unitary_state" title="Unitary state">unitary</a> <a href="/wiki/Parliamentary_system" title="Parliamentary system">parliamentary</a> <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_monarchy" title="Constitutional monarchy">constitutional monarchy</a> with an <a href="/wiki/Emperor_of_Japan" title="Emperor of Japan">Emperor</a> and an elected legislature called the <a href="/wiki/National_Diet" title="National Diet">National Diet</a>.\n</p><p>The  <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign state</a> of Japan  is a member of the <a href="/wiki/Association_of_Southeast_Asian_Nations#ASEAN_Plus_Three_and_Six" title="Association of Southeast Asian Nations">ASEAN Plus mechanism</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">UN</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Organisation_for_Economic_Co-operation_and_Development" class="mw-redirect" title="Organisation for Economic Co-operation and Development">OECD</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Group_of_Seven" title="Group of Seven">G7</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Group_of_Eight" title="Group of Eight">G8</a> and the <a href="/wiki/G20" title="G20">G20</a>\xe2\x80\x94and is considered a <a href="/wiki/Great_power" title="Great power">great power</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Balance_of_Power_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Balance_of_Power-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Joshua_Baron_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Joshua_Baron-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> The country has the world\'s third-largest <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(nominal)" title="List of countries by GDP (nominal)">economy by nominal GDP</a> and the world\'s fourth-largest <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP)">economy by purchasing power parity</a>. It is also the world\'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_exports" title="List of countries by exports">fourth-largest exporter</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_imports" title="List of countries by imports">fourth-largest importer</a>.\n</p><p>The country benefits from a highly skilled workforce and is among the most highly educated countries in the world, with one of the highest percentages of its citizens holding a tertiary education degree.<sup id="cite_ref-OECD_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OECD-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Although Japan has officially <a href="/wiki/Article_9_of_the_Japanese_Constitution" title="Article 9 of the Japanese Constitution">renounced its right to declare war</a>, it maintains a <a href="/wiki/Japan_Self-Defense_Forces" title="Japan Self-Defense Forces">modern military</a> with the world\'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_military_expenditures" title="List of countries by military expenditures">eighth-largest military budget</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> used for <a href="/wiki/Self-defense" title="Self-defense">self-defense</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peacekeeping" title="Peacekeeping">peacekeeping</a> roles. It ranked as the world\'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_Military_Strength_Index" title="List of countries by Military Strength Index">fourth most-powerful military</a> in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-CreditSuisse2015_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CreditSuisse2015-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Japan is a highly <a href="/wiki/Developed_country" title="Developed country">developed country</a> with a very high standard of living and <a href="/wiki/Human_Development_Index" title="Human Development Index">Human Development Index</a>. Its population enjoys the <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_life_expectancy" title="List of countries by life expectancy">highest life expectancy</a> and the third lowest <a href="/wiki/Infant_mortality" title="Infant mortality">infant mortality</a> rate in the world, but is experiencing issues due to an aging population and low birthrate. Japan is renowned for its historical and extensive <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Japan" title="Cinema of Japan">cinema</a>, influential <a href="/wiki/Music_of_Japan" title="Music of Japan">music</a> industry, <a href="/wiki/Anime" title="Anime">anime</a>, <a href="/wiki/Video_gaming_in_Japan" title="Video gaming in Japan">video gaming</a>, rich <a href="/wiki/Japanese_cuisine" title="Japanese cuisine">cuisine</a> and its major contributions to science and modern-day technology.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Table_A.17_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Table_A.17-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" class="toclevel-2 tocsection-32"><a href="#Languages"><span class="tocnumber">9.3</span> <span class="toctext">Languages</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-33"><a href="#Problems"><span class="tocnumber">9.4</span> <span class="toctext">Problems</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-34"><a href="#Education"><span class="tocnumber">10</span> <span class="toclevel-2 tocsection-40"><a href="#Cinema"><span class="tocnumber">12.4</span> <span class="toctext">Cinema</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-41"><a href="#Etiquette"><span class="tocnumber">12.5</span> <span class="toctext">Etiquette</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-42"><a href="#Music"><span class="tocnumber">12.6</span> <span class="toctext">Music</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-43"><a href="#Literature"><span class="tocnumber">12.7</span> <span class="toctext">Literature</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-44"><a href="#Philosophy"><span class="tocnumber">12.8</span> <span class="toctext">Philosophy</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-45"><a href="#Cuisine"><span class="tocnumber">12.9</span> <span class="toctext">Cuisine</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-46"><a href="#Holidays"><span class="tocnumber">12.10</span> <span class="toctext">Holidays</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-47"><a href="#Festivals"><span class="tocnumber">12.11</span> <span class="toctext">Festivals</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-48"><a href="#Sports"><span class="tocnumber">12.12</span> <span class="toctext">Sports</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-49"><a href="#Video_Gaming"><span
